  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_713bd029-4ab2-43b1-9810-1cd51b457e6c'
      });

<div id="review_648677263" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648677263" />
    <a title="Tina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6383594-tina"><img alt="Tina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371867364p2/6383594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648677263?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tina" href="/user/show/6383594-tina">Tina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648677263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18263026820277137788"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>The <i>Fallen Crest High</i> Series is like junk food. You know you shouldn't have it because it's bad for you, but this ends up happening anyways.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962426.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm a lot happier with how <i>Fallen Crest Public</i> turned out compared to the last book. Sam has some of her spunk back though her emotional side is still there. I'm happy she has both (heck, I'd prefer it if she has both), but still a tiny bit unsatisfied with how she is. If I could accurately describe it, I'd say she's roughly 40% IDGAF Sam from Book 1,</span>
  <span id="freeText18263026820277137788" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>The <i>Fallen Crest High</i> Series is like junk food. You know you shouldn't have it because it's bad for you, but this ends up happening anyways.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962426.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm a lot happier with how <i>Fallen Crest Public</i> turned out compared to the last book. Sam has some of her spunk back though her emotional side is still there. I'm happy she has both (heck, I'd prefer it if she has both), but still a tiny bit unsatisfied with how she is. If I could accurately describe it, I'd say she's roughly 40% IDGAF Sam from Book 1, 50% emotional Sam from Book 2, and 10% New Sam with a big moral compass. She can get a tiny bit annoying sometimes in the book, but she's mostly bearable if not likable in some parts. I think it's safe to say you'll definitely love her when IDGAF Sam comes out.<br><br>As for Mason and Logan...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962427.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They're sexy as always. Logan's still the hot, caring jokester and Mason is still the sexy, caring badass.<br><br>As for the romance between Mason and Sam, I'll explain it in strictly gif form how hot, sexy, and sweet it is.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962428.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962429.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962430.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962431.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962432.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>And the drama. The book is a delicious dessert on the outside with a whole lotta OMG on the inside.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388954063ra/7962433.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The story isn't as crazy as the previous book, but that doesn't mean there's not a lot of shit going on. This one pretty much centers on high school drama with a dash of romantic drama and a sprinkle of violent drama. Just be prepared because some of the stuff going on is like a car accident you can't look away from.<br><br>And the ending. I'm not exactly a fan of the ending because it seemed like it was going for a shocker dramatic ending but it didn't for me. I won't say who for spoilers but was I the only one who wasn't surprised that he loves her? Maybe it's from reading so many romantic novels that I'm used to sniffing out this type of stuff, but I thought it was pretty obvious he had feelings for her (especially since it's pointed out a few times despite being joked about). And because I wasn't really surprised, the ending pretty much fell flat for me as it was anti-climactic.<br><br>However, I enjoyed the book overall. Still hoping to see more badass Sam and see a better execution of her dealing with her family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Really? New dad's just gone and you suddenly throw in issues with David in a high school drama centered story? Don't get me wrong, I'm happy that they've worked things out but it seemed inconsistent to suddenly bring that issue up <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. If you're debating whether or not to read the 3rd book, I say do it. It might not be as good as the first one, but it's definitely better than the second. You'll be disappointed in a few parts of the storyline, but I think, for the most part, you'll be satisfied. That being said, I'm curious to see what happens in the next book.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="18263026820277137788" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText11635379159115512209" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388373609i/7813366._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Note:</u> Not really a review, just some random ramblings of mine. Kate’s knocked off her pedestal and how to deal with ex-drama queen bee is a major problem.<br><br><b>
  <i>“New definition to the phrase ‘dumb bitch.’”</i>
</b><br><br>2. The Broudou brothers are out to get Mason and anything and everything he holds dear.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You fuck with who I love, and I fuck with you.”</i>
</b><br><br>3. Don’t forget the messed up, headache-inducing, bang-my-head-on-the-wall family dynamics from book 2! Although they play a lesser role and aren’t the main focus of this book, the <s>crazy gorillas</s> parents are an influence.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Helen was a saner version of Analise.”</i>

Tijan totally TIJANED you!<br><br><u>Me:</u> ...............<br><br><u>Book Me:</u> Hey, you okay?<br><br><u>Me:</u> Yeah, totally fine. Just...having a moment and absorbing it all in.<br><br>So yeah, a third installment filled with wicked turns and twists and plot punches you’ll never see coming?   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656106407" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/656106407?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>

          marked it as i-m-a-quitter




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=the-hype-is-a-lie">the-hype-is-a-lie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=jump-off-a-cliff-hanger">jump-off-a-cliff-hanger</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer656106407" class="readable"

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4841295427179886005"><b>"Turning my head to the side, his lips were there and they opened for me. I needed him. Sweeping my tongue against his lips, I tasted what was mine. He was mine. All of him was mine."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388534417ra/7862202.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>See when I see that word "mine" I think it means "mine" personally not "hers" because the way I look at if I'm reading the word then it means it's "mine!" Thank goodness you understand every thing I just said because the "it" is Mason and I'm so happy he's MINE!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>My Loves</i>
</b><br/><br/>Well obviously Mason and Logan Kade...*si</span>
  <span id="freeText4841295427179886005" style="display:none"><b>"Turning my head to the side, his lips were there and they opened for me. I needed him. Sweeping my tongue against his lips, I tasted what was mine. He was mine. All of him was mine."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388534417ra/7862202.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>See when I see that word "mine" I think it means "mine" personally not "hers" because the way I look at if I'm reading the word then it means it's "mine!" Thank goodness you understand every thing I just said because the "it" is Mason and I'm so happy he's MINE!!!<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>My Loves</i>
</b><br><br>Well obviously Mason and Logan Kade...*sigh*. They are just to lickable to even describe properly!! My parents are still married but <b>WOW</b> I could have used some step brothers like these two!!!!!<br><br><br>This author always leaves wanting more even though I had some slight issues with this one.<br><br>I'm so greatful that I didn't have to endure the crazy batshit behavior from Analise in this book.........woman you need <b>HELP you PSYCHO!!</b><br><br>These books are fast paced and quick, they aren't easy to just find a stopping point and end it for the night. This definitely delivered on that point. I devoured this book in a day and half:)<br><br>Samantha "Sam" I love you because they love you so much. Also I was proud when you stood up for yourself to Kate.....slamming some ones face in a table is always therapeutic when your mad!!! <b>PERFECT!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388534701ra/7862265.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>My likes</i>
</b><br><br>I enjoyed the new secondary characters we were introduced to especially Malinda Decraw.....she was <b>AWESOME!!!!!</b> I love her!!!!<br><br>The fragile relationship that is trying to be patched by Sam and her Dad, David, I've always liked him through out this series. I felt he had handed the short straw in the divorce.<br><br>I like the fact that Heather is sticking around she's shaping up to be a decent friend.<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>My *head tilting sideways* with a frowny face...yes it's the dislikes</i>
</b><br><br>This hurts my heart to say this because I love this author but this book just didn't flow good to me:(<br><br>There were multiple times the dialogue between characters didn't even make sense....I would have to reread the interaction because it made no sense or the response that was made was not even revlavent to what was asked or said:(<br><br>I don't know it just seemed rushed....I don't mean the book or the storyline just the book as a whole.<br><br>Oh and the diabolical plan.....just a <b>WEE</b> bit over the top but that's just my opinion.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388535213ra/7862369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Now I'm taking a *deep breath* in and out because this is one of my favorite series and I hate being critical about it. <br><br>Now with all that being said don't get me wrong I will still devour the next book in this series because <b>DAMN</b>......we were left with a <b>HUGE cliff!!!!!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388535269ra/7862377.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>HUGE PEOPLE!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><br><br>Overall if you love this series you will love this book because quite frankly how could you not love anything Mason and Logan Kade are in:)<br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_755897627" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755897627" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755897627?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755897627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3078769836694823"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>I love Tijan’s books and I loved Fallen Crest High series, however, and yes I have to put that “tiny” however there and major sigh to the fact, Fallen Crest Public is NOT the last book in the series. I would describe book 1, Fallen Crest High as the pilot of the series and with each book that is release, is kind of a like an episode as in, each book has a major obstacle that needs to be overcome. In book 2, Fallen Crest family, the main obstacle was Sam’s crazy mom and in book 3, Fallen C</span>
  <span id="freeText3078769836694823" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>I love Tijan’s books and I loved Fallen Crest High series, however, and yes I have to put that “tiny” however there and major sigh to the fact, Fallen Crest Public is NOT the last book in the series. I would describe book 1, Fallen Crest High as the pilot of the series and with each book that is release, is kind of a like an episode as in, each book has a major obstacle that needs to be overcome. In book 2, Fallen Crest family, the main obstacle was Sam’s crazy mom and in book 3, Fallen Crest Public, the main obstacle is Kate.<br><br>Mason, Logan and Sam all live with Nate. It’s the last semester of high school before Mason goes to college. Also, Sam is going to school with Mason and Logan now. Not everyone in school, especially the girls and especially Kate is okay with Sam.<br><br>First off, I loved the main theme, “damsel in distress”, yup, I love it, I eat it up and I don’t care how much you want a “strong” Heroine. Sam is still strong, but sometimes a strong Heroine needs to be saved by a crazy over protective Hero. The star of the book would be Mason. If you could create an alpha high schooler with sexy looks and charming personality, my money would be on Mason.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/VoYWIER" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389016963i/7971100.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I have a major book boyfriend crush on Mason Kade. Don’t worry there’s plenty of Logan action for all those who are team Logan. One of the main things I love about the series is the adorable relationship Mason, Logan and Sam have with each other. I think its super cute, it makes me smile and it’s something I eat up.<br><br>Kate is a crazy bia and strikes a lot of terror and there are many difficulties because of her. I like this, it creates nice tension, but none of the pull-you-hair-out kind. There has to be a major villain in every book and Tijan created one I loved to hate.<br><br>Now, let’s get to the things that did not work out for me.<br><br>I fairly enjoyed FCP because I’m a HUGE fan of Tijan’s writing, but I am disappointed to say this one missed the mark just a bit for me. The writing was a bit drawn out, in the sense, I did skim a few pages here and there. Also, THERE ARE SO MANY FUCKING CHARACTERS. I felt like I need to create a spread sheet of who dated who, who was related to whom and who were friends and who were enemies. <br><br>The biggest draw back of the book for me was the ending. For a few reasons, first I thought the series was ending, but it didn’t. I thought the ending mirrored a lot like another book I have previous read, so it didn’t seem very original. I did not like the direction of the ending because it goes against the dynamic of the book (again for me). With that said, I will not be continuing the series. As much as I love the Kade brothers, I just don’t want to see where the story is going to go.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/KUAMUHf" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389016963i/7971101.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think Tijan broke my heart, but I still am a major fan.<br><br>I just have to say, my “issues” aren’t really issues. In all sense, I think if you are a fan of the series, you will enjoy it and will more than likely be very content. I’m just the odd duck on this one. <br><br><i>ARC and images provided by the author</i><br><br>Series Order<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134551.Fallen_Crest_High__Fallen_Crest_High___1_" title="Fallen Crest High (Fallen Crest High, #1) by Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1370230318s/16134551.jpg" alt="Fallen Crest High (Fallen Crest High, #1) by Tijan" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/725697484%22" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B009ZOZP0W/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B009ZOZP0W&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17191012.Fallen_Crest_Family__Fallen_Crest_High___2_" title="Fallen Crest Family (Fallen Crest High, #2) by Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1370197330s/17191012.jpg" alt="Fallen Crest Family (Fallen Crest High, #2) by Tijan" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/729529755" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00DHT1OOM/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00DHT1OOM&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383518499i/6584564.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>More here - &gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/">http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot....</a></span>

  <span id="freeText13000022077790411330" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*It was kinda a bust; I was bored*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
  <br>
  <i>This review is purely for me and might contain spoilers and facts from the book to keep myself in the known at all time. It's also <b>long</b> and somewhat detailed.</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527238949i/25594311.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 25.05.2018</u>
</b><br>We're back with <b>Samantha ‘Sam’ Jacquelyn Strattan</b> (18) and her boyfriend/future-stepbrother, <b>Mason ‘Mase’ James Kade</b> (18). Sam is now starting Fallen Crest Public High along side the Kade brothers, but now everyones is happy about that. Sam gets targeted by the The Tommy P's/Princesses who are determined to remove her. Then there's also the threat of the Broudou brothers; words out that Mason has a girlfriend and Budd's out to hurt her. First they gotta find out who she is. <b>Overall, it's not as bad as second book</b>, however it's still far from a great read. Sure, I still enjoyed it to a degree, but there's something huge that's missing from this book (and previous book), and that something is nagging at me. I do believe that it's the missing depth. I'm kinda looking forward to be completely done with this series. I do still love Mason though; I sure do want him for myself...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Principal Green surveyed the crowd in the hallway, shaking his head at the same time. “How is it that you two command so much attention in this school? I’ve never met another person, much less a pair of brothers that can compete with the level of power you hold over my student population.”<br>Logan shrugged. “We’re cool, an inspiration to others.”<br>A smattering of laughter started again.<br>Principal Green drawled, “I highly doubt that.”<br>“It’s true. We’re like a walking Hallmark card, full of quotes and bible verses. We make people feel like they’ve been touched by an angel.”<br>“Oh, shit,” someone laughed.<br>Another commented, “He makes people feel touched all right.”<br>A third snorted, “And not from anything angelic.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br><i>I've put these in a spoilers tag simply because it's a long as list.</i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>↦ <b>Logan Kade</b> (17?), Mason's brother. And they go to Fallen Crest Public High school and both brothers played for the school football team. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Tate tells Sam that Logan is in love with her at the end of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>↦ <b>Nate Monson</b> (18), Mason's best friend and Logan's friend. Nate's parents were movie directors.<br>↦ <b>James Kade</b>, the Kade brothers father. Not a good father.<br>↦ <b>Analise ‘Lise’ Strattan</b>, Sam's mother. Bad, bad mother.<br>↦ <b>David Strattan</b> (45), Sam's father (though not biological father) and coach for the football team at a private school; Fallen Crest Academy. He should've fought more for Sam. Proven to her that, though he isn't her biological father, he <i>is</i> her father as he raised her.<br>↦ <b>Garrett Brickshire</b>, Sam's biological father, the hotshot lawyer from Boston. Seems like a cool dude, though perhaps a selfish one?<br>↦ <b>Helen Malbourne</b>, the Kade brothers mother. Not sure how I feel about this woman. She is kinda a bitch, like Sam's mother. A different kind of bitch?<br>↦ <b>Jeffrey ‘Jeff’ Sallaway</b>, Sam's ex. They dated for three years. <b>Jessica ‘Jess’ Larsen</b> and <b>Lydia Thompson</b>, Sam's <s>friends</s> from school. Jess has been fooling around with Jeff behind Sam's back for over two years, Lydia hid it. <b>Jill Flatten</b>, an enemy of Sam, now dating Jeff after Sam broke up with him. Lydia tries to be a better friend to Sam eventually, Jessica still hates her.<br>↦ <b>Adam Quinn</b>, Academy team’s quarterback. Has a crush on Sam. Uses Becky to get to her. <b>Ashley DeCortts</b>, his ex-girlfriend.<br>↦ <b>Rebecca ‘Becky’ Sallaway</b>, Jeff’s cousin only through marriage. She were Sam's somewhat friend, until she stopped talking to her. She has a major crush on Adam, but think herself not worthy of him. Has now a boyfriend named <b>Raz</b>.<br>↦ <b>Malinda Decraw</b>, She was the single mother of Mark Decraw; one of Becky’s termed Academy Elite. He was co-captain. She seems interested in David; they start dating.<br>↦ <b>Miranda Stewart</b>, Fallen Academy’s elite queen bee. <b>Cassandra Sullivan</b>, <b>Emily Connsway</b>, <b>Peter Glasburg</b>, <b>Amelia White</b>, <b>Mark Decraw</b>; members of the group. Adam is in it too. - Miranda's with Peter. Cass wants Adam. Amelia and Mark seems to be dating.<br>↦ <b>Marissa</b>, a good friend of Mason. He protective of her because he's the reason she had to switch schools a couple years ago.<br>↦ <b>Tate Sullivan</b>, Logan's ex of two years. She tried to come between Mason and his brother; she used Logan to get to Mason. That’s why he hate the bitch, but Logan still loves her. Which is why he has a soft spot for her. <b>Tanya</b>, Tate' cousin. <br>↦ <b>Heather Jax</b>, her brother, <b>Brandon Jax</b>. Their father owns the diner side of their humble abode inside; a run-down dive/a bar called Manny. <b>Anne</b> and <b>Lily</b>, waitresses at Manny's, along side with Sam, who starts working there. Heather's friends <b>Channing Monroe </b>; they seem to have a thing and he who goes to Roussou High school.<br>↦ The Tommy P's/Princesses (Heather's name for the mean bitches); <b>Kate</b> was the ring leader. <b>Parker</b> was her sidekick, but there was another twosome that made up the core group of their four; <b>Natalie</b> and <b>Jasmine</b>. Ethan Fischer, the fourth in command after Mason, Logan, and Nate. Strauss, as friend of the boys. They all go to Fallen Crest Public High school. <br>↦ The Broudou brothers; there are three of them. <b>Brett</b> and <b>Budd</b> are the ones Sam has met so far. Two are seniors this year, twins, and they have a third little brother in Sam grade. But all of them hate Kade because of their sister, <b>Shannon Broudou</b> who lied and claimed that that Kade met her at a party, slept with her, and never called her back. They think he treated her like trash. Truth is that nothing happened with Kade and her. They are all from Roussou.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Budd ends up in jail thanks to Sam, Brett declares peace. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Next time you’re pissed at me, can you do me a favor?”<br>“Yeah?”<br>“Don’t go to Logan.” His eyes moved to mine and held them captive. My mouth dropped open as he stole my breath away. That hand went back into my chest and squeezed, but it was a different pain this time. It was from the pain I caused him.<br>I nodded. “I’m sorry.”<br>“He’s my brother. You’re my other half. I can’t …”<br>When he struggled for words, I reached for his hand. I started to go to him, but my ribs protested, so I gripped his hand as tight as I could. “I won’t ever do that again. I promise.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Young Adult) Contemorary Romance.<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Three.<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, but there's been hints. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not really; Mason uses Kate to put a target on her back and away from Sam. He does kiss her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Mason Kade.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably not. <br><b>New Rating</b> - 2.5 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 22.08.15</u>
</b><br>Meh, not bad, but far from a great re-read. Still 3 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>First read: 22.05.14</u>
</b><br>I do love Mason. Other than that, the book is a bit boring.<br><b>Rating: 3 stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232475666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16857684359426455226"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426867945i/14112571.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>It's not fair that I'm angry right now. I thought I was finally hitting a stride with the Fallen Crest series. I <i>thought</i> I was learning to enjoy the ride enough to cave and ignore the repetitive writing plus editing flaws because the drama was exciting and addictive. I actually kind of liked book 2 (which I still haven't reviewed yet because I had to jump ahead and unload my pent-up frustration over book 3). <br/><br/><i>Why</i> couldn't the sketchy behavior have been limited to the "enemies" of Mason, Logan, an</span>
  <span id="freeText16857684359426455226" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426867945i/14112571.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It's not fair that I'm angry right now. I thought I was finally hitting a stride with the Fallen Crest series. I <i>thought</i> I was learning to enjoy the ride enough to cave and ignore the repetitive writing plus editing flaws because the drama was exciting and addictive. I actually kind of liked book 2 (which I still haven't reviewed yet because I had to jump ahead and unload my pent-up frustration over book 3). <br><br><i>Why</i> couldn't the sketchy behavior have been limited to the "enemies" of Mason, Logan, and Samantha? <i>Why</i> did I have to start liking the male leads, only to have it all snatched away when their bad behavior became inexcusable (again)?<br><br>It's NOT okay that Logan and Mason <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[threw Kate to Budd, <i>knowing</i> that he was going to hurt her. I'm guessing that they probably knew (if only subconsciously) that she might be raped. But even if they didn't know how far it would go, the fact that they would set a girl up to be physically beaten by a male takes them out of the running for "hot" male leads. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Doesn't anyone else get this? These two guys <i>shouldn't</i> be viable romance leads now. <i>Especially</i> while starring in a high school series with a younger target age range. This is the worst possible shit that anyone would want their daughter reading and aspiring to date. Extreme questionable behavior should be reserved for adult anti-heroes...or at the very least, younger male leads who aren't considered swoon-worthy. Broken people who need help - fine. Guys who are fawned over by every available female - not fine. <br><br>Saving Samantha is NOT a good enough excuse. ANY decent human being would not throw another person to the wolves like that. If they'd set Kate up to have a go-round with another chick, whatever. She would've gotten what was coming to her for the stunt she pulled in the bathroom. But what happened goes beyond basic revenge payback. <br><br>Again, there were enough side characters in the book who could have been as evil as they wanted to be. I just don't want to see young male leads being swooned over when they are prone to downright disgusting behavior.<br><br>Remember : Kate was set up to be <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[beaten and/or raped. By a guy. This was not a chick fight. This was a life-altering crime. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And Logan and Mason were going to ignore it happening. <br><br>THIS IS NOT OKAY. AND IT'S NOT EXCUSABLE FOR THE SAKE OF ENTERTAINMENT VALUE.<br><br>Logan and Mason : Use your brains, kids. Find another way to save the girl you love. <br><br><br><br>(And it sure was awfully convenient that Sam just happened to be the only person in town jogging by at that exact moment when everything started to go down with Kate.<br><br>And it was even more disgusting that the convenience store guy did jack shit about what was happening.) <br><br>And I know I mentioned the repetitive stuff, but I'm really tired of everyone pressing kisses to Sam's forehead, temple, and shoulder. There was one instance where it happened 3 times within the span of a page and a half. And...for a girl who can run, she sure gets carried around a lot. Must be that all-consuming addiction thing. <br><br><br><br>Gah. I really was enjoying this book too, up until M&amp;L went back onto my shit list. <br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16857684359426455226" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648947454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16887432351298668868"><b> Pre-book review: </b><br/><br/>Eagerly waiting for the book! BUT please, Bring back the old Samantha. The one who was all bold and smart. not the one full with emotions...I'm happy she has emotions, but still... the old one was better. And what's with Nate? I don't like him and I do NOT trust him! :/<br/><br/>*******************************<br/><b> Post-book Review: 31st Dec. </b><br/><br/>First of all I'd like to thank Tijan for making my 31st December so freaking awesome! You and your books are totally awesome and I love you a lot!<br/><br/>Readin</span>
  <span id="freeText16887432351298668868" style="display:none"><b> Pre-book review: </b><br /><br />Eagerly waiting for the book! BUT please, Bring back the old Samantha. The one who was all bold and smart. not the one full with emotions...I'm happy she has emotions, but still... the old one was better. And what's with Nate? I don't like him and I do NOT trust him! :/<br /><br />*******************************<br /><b> Post-book Review: 31st Dec. </b><br /><br />First of all I'd like to thank Tijan for making my 31st December so freaking awesome! You and your books are totally awesome and I love you a lot!<br /><br />Reading Fallen Crest Public was like riding on a roller coaster--up down left right. Not a single page left me unsatisfied. It was very much thrilling.<br /><br />Mason<br />His POV was really a great insight to his mind. I got to know a lot of things about him which I couldn't in the first two books. He really is protective of Sam and would do 'anything' (deep emphasis on anything) for her, which he did by ruining Kate. He is too much observant and really caring. But Man! The way he had planned out on outcasting Kate was just... *I'm speechless* He is an evil mastermind! I'm sorry Sam but I guess I am in love with him too. :P<br /><br />Logan<br />Same as ever. He loved and protected Sam too. I was nervous when I read the part where Sam was literally throwing herself on him. But good old brother did nothing. I understand why he hates Nate because he wasn't that close to his brother as Nate was.<br /><br />Samantha.<br />Girl got her 'bitchiness' back in the third book. Yeah, she was an emotional mess but c'mon the girl did stand for herself and every human has to show emotions once in a while. I hated that psychopath Kate and her followers. How in the hell could she beat up Sam like that?! I did cry a bit when she felt hurt watching Kate and Mason together. I liked her loyalty towards Heather. But one good thing about her: She is not bad. She did help Kate, the same girl who knocked her out, with a big BOOM. <br /><br />Nate.<br />Lol he did seem shady and now I know the reason why. He seems like a good guy but I still don't understand that bond between him and Mase.<br /><br /><br /><br />The plot was awesome. Tijan captured each emotions and all the situations in detail which made me connect to everyone. <br />The story ended with a BANG! and a very unsettling confession. <br />Now that the ending was incomplete I guess there's gonna be more adventures of The Fallen Crest people. <br /><br />Can't wait for the fourth book! :(<br />This series I recommend to all. If you haven't read it, then do! You'll love it!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2301323358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17930589067191305815">DNF at 26%<br/><br/>I am so over this. <br/><br/>Nothing has changed. We get the same conversations and situations over and over. There is no difference between the two first books of the series and this one. We are reading the same book repeatedly. <br/> I can't stand any longer all the bitchiness, meanness, randomness and plane badness of all the characters. The reflections and dialogues of the characters are illogical, they make no sense whatsoever and piss me off. The characters are an example of bad decision making</span>
  <span id="freeText17930589067191305815" style="display:none">DNF at 26%<br /><br />I am so over this. <br /><br />Nothing has changed. We get the same conversations and situations over and over. There is no difference between the two first books of the series and this one. We are reading the same book repeatedly. <br /> I can't stand any longer all the bitchiness, meanness, randomness and plane badness of all the characters. The reflections and dialogues of the characters are illogical, they make no sense whatsoever and piss me off. The characters are an example of bad decision making and of the bad sides of humans. <br />It is shameful how the teenage girls are portrait here over and over again. The boys are entitled cowards, all bark and no bite. It is disgusting to see. I am so fed up with al this I can't continue any longer reading this series, it is depressing. <b>No more</b>.<br /><br />WRONG!<br /><br />P.S.: I do not recommend this series.<br /><br />Book 1:<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2270306442?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Crest High</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2300437679?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Crest Family</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17930589067191305815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

That was absolutely... perfect!<br><br>Thank God, everything found the right place at the end...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422641940i/13529114.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>...except that something fucked up everything at the end and now i'm sitting here alone and i'm wondering who will be hurting in the end!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422641820ra/13529094.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Please, please, Tijan!!! Protect my lovely Mason!!!</i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1299240513?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18892770-fallen-crest-public">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1299240513" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5468691084632950238">In this third book in the series, Sam finds herself, yet again, pitted against the "mean girls" at her new school. When Mason ruins these girls social standing by "exiling" them, their tactics only become more cruel. With the ringleader focusing all her anger on Sam, tensions build steadily until they finally attack. These girls are vicious, brutal and all-around scary!<br/><br/>Mason and Logan continue to be overly protective of Sam, but this book sees their good intentions cause some damage. More and mo</span>
  <span id="freeText5468691084632950238" style="display:none">In this third book in the series, Sam finds herself, yet again, pitted against the "mean girls" at her new school. When Mason ruins these girls social standing by "exiling" them, their tactics only become more cruel. With the ringleader focusing all her anger on Sam, tensions build steadily until they finally attack. These girls are vicious, brutal and all-around scary!<br /><br />Mason and Logan continue to be overly protective of Sam, but this book sees their good intentions cause some damage. More and more, Sam is left in the dark as their plotting takes on a secretive nature. When everything finally comes to light, I think she let the guys off easy, especially Mason.<br /><br />After everything, Sam continues to be compassionate and merciful. She even goes out of her way to save a girl that had tormented her for weeks. I was blown away by her kindness and humanity after everything she had been put through. She had a chance for revenge, but she took the high ground, despite knowing that the other girl would have walked away and left her to suffer if the tables had been turned.<br /><br />Three books in and this series still has my attention! I'm loving all of this high school drama that would normally drive me crazy. It's a bit far-fetched, but highly entertaining! On to the next one...</span>
  <a data-text-id="5468691084632950238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1149523428792207161">Tijan is officially my 'go to' author. Reading her books is like curling up with my favorite blanket and settling in for the night. Except there is no sleeping because I'm trapped between the pages and it's a great trapped. It's opening up a book (turning on your kindle) and your body sags and you sink into the words on the page with a sigh. That is my Tijan experience so far and I love her for giving me that. <br/></span>

Hope she opens up more in the next book!!<br><br>And Tijan...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388471197ra/7844049.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435911ra/880863.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388471197ra/7844050.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously... <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388471197ra/7844051.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But while I wait..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388471197ra/7844052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_692499684" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692499684" />
    <a title="Crazies R Us Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20727250-crazies-r-us-book-blog"><img alt="Crazies R Us Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395277652p2/20727250.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692499684?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Crazies R Us Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crazies R Us Book Blog" href="/user/show/20727250-crazies-r-us-book-blog">Crazies R Us Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692499684" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13141798497715105243">*CAMI'S REVIEW*<br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382317141i/5814311.png' alt=' photo 5_star_review33151521_std_zps063314ab.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>5+++++ "Crazie" Stars!!!! <br/>OMG!! If you thought the first two books in the series were great, wait until you get a ahold of this one!!!!!! <br/>"Badass" Sam is back with a vengeance! And there are so many changes in Sam's life now that she is attending FCP. The drama in this book is off the charts and the vibe at FCP is without a doubt, VERY different from the Academy. <br/>Now attending Fallen Crest Public and being Mason Kade's girlfriend, Sam knew she would have a target on h</span>
  <span id="freeText13141798497715105243" style="display:none">*CAMI'S REVIEW*<br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382317141i/5814311.png" alt=" photo 5_star_review33151521_std_zps063314ab.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5+++++ "Crazie" Stars!!!! <br>OMG!! If you thought the first two books in the series were great, wait until you get a ahold of this one!!!!!! <br>"Badass" Sam is back with a vengeance! And there are so many changes in Sam's life now that she is attending FCP. The drama in this book is off the charts and the vibe at FCP is without a doubt, VERY different from the Academy. <br>Now attending Fallen Crest Public and being Mason Kade's girlfriend, Sam knew she would have a target on her back. Add into the mix, Kate and her bitch crew, (oh and don't forget Tate) and Sam has got her hands full! <br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388365925i/7811299._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo FCPCAMI2REVIEW1229194417_zpscc1aa98e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> I expected Kate of course to be bitchy and cause trouble, but not to go to the extent she does. ( I should've known better after reading AWNC) . But OMG! These FCP kids are ruthless! <br>Of course Mason and Logan are not about to let anything happen to her! <br>I was so happy to get Mason's POV!!! When reading it, there are two sides to him that come through loud and clear. He's calculated...the wheels are always turning and he knows exactly what he's doing! And he's vulnerable.....ESPECIALLY when it comes to Sam.<br>This series is without a doubt one of the best I have ever read! The kind that sticks with you long after you read it and one you don't have to go back and read the previous books in the series to remember what's been happening. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388365925i/7811300._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo FCPDIAMOND21229194722_zpsd537436a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are twists and turns that will leave you speechless! Utterly SPEECHLESS I tell you! I won't reveal any spoilers though. I think it would ruin the story. But I will tell you, I LOVED every minute of it and my stomach was filled with butterflies throughout most of the book! Yes it is THAT GOOD!! Well played Tijan. Well played!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13141798497715105243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dRCnrdtboMbDVfDiSP7KfD128azPhzlTCyLHJUa/Hl9hYhwzkpfDNste23XwEUNwxyTI/wRtA7MPTG2N5WGb0g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FU3gs3ZMJHKJSPiETJsm6K7fuTTtsH3xuW8qMC33KV8BP1stP4BHgoFD0xP0dK/kVI2AZyZaRxG9AYCYjims0g==')})
  }
